# Band 2 Science Templates — Strand 1: Life Sciences & Scientific Inquiry

*Note: This file contains both the Scientific Inquiry (SE) cross-cutting progression capacities and the Strand 1 Life Sciences (LS) capacities.*

## SE2a: Sensory Observation

### Encounter Level (Physical Observation)

**SE2a-1A: Encounter Variation A**
```json
{
  "capacity_id": "SE2a",
  "strand": 1,
  "band": 2,
  "cognitive_level": 1,
  "variation_id": "A",
  "task_type": "Encounter (Observation)",
  "risk_level": "Risk_Level_A",
  "safety_warning": "Safe for independent work. Do not eat unknown plants.",
  "scientific_materials": [
    "Ugandan fruit (e.g., jackfruit)",
    "leaves",
    "stone"
  ],
  "acceptable_alternatives": [
    "any local fruit",
    "grass",
    "wood"
  ],
  "parent_prompt": "Variation A: Parent guides child to directly observe Sensory Observation using Ugandan fruit (e.g., jackfruit). \"Look closely at this. What do you notice?\"",
  "success_condition": "Child successfully completes the observation or explanation.",
  "failure_condition": "Child needs guidance. Parent asks guiding questions.",
  "reasoning_check": "What do you see, hear, or feel?",
  "context_variants": {
    "default": {
      "names": [
        "Alex",
        "Sam",
        "Pat"
      ],
      "settings": [
        "park",
        "school",
        "store"
      ],
      "food": [
        "apples",
        "bread",
        "milk"
      ]
    },
    "ug": {
      "names": [
        "Amara",
        "Tendo",
        "Azie"
      ],
      "settings": [
        "Kampala market",
        "village",
        "garden",
        "savanna",
        "wetland"
      ],
      "food": [
        "matooke",
        "mangoes",
        "chapati",
        "jackfruit"
      ]
    }
  },
  "repetition_arc": {
    "execution_count": 3,
    "endurance": "noise_injection",
    "milestone": "M"
  },
  "observable_phenomenon": "Direct physical observation of sensory observation"
}
```

### Execute Level (Experiment)

**SE2a-2A: Execute Variation A**
```json
{
  "capacity_id": "SE2a",
  "strand": 1,
  "band": 2,
  "cognitive_level": 2,
  "variation_id": "A",
  "task_type": "Execute (Experiment/Sorting)",
  "risk_level": "Risk_Level_A",
  "safety_warning": "Safe for independent work. Do not eat unknown plants.",
  "scientific_materials": [
    "Ugandan fruit (e.g., jackfruit)",
    "leaves",
    "stone"
  ],
  "acceptable_alternatives": [
    "any local fruit",
    "grass",
    "wood"
  ],
  "parent_prompt": "Variation A: \"Use the Ugandan fruit (e.g., jackfruit) to test Sensory Observation. Sort the results into two piles.\"",
  "success_condition": "Child successfully completes the observation or explanation.",
  "failure_condition": "Child needs guidance. Parent asks guiding questions.",
  "reasoning_check": "How did you record your data?",
  "context_variants": {
    "default": {
      "names": [
        "Alex",
        "Sam",
        "Pat"
      ],
      "settings": [
        "park",
        "school",
        "store"
      ],
      "food": [
        "apples",
        "bread",
        "milk"
      ]
    },
    "ug": {
      "names": [
        "Amara",
        "Tendo",
        "Azie"
      ],
      "settings": [
        "Kampala market",
        "village",
        "garden",
        "savanna",
        "wetland"
      ],
      "food": [
        "matooke",
        "mangoes",
        "chapati",
        "jackfruit"
      ]
    }
  },
  "repetition_arc": {
    "execution_count": 3,
    "endurance": "noise_injection",
    "milestone": "M"
  },
  "parent_rubric": [
    {
      "criterion": "Did the child safely handle materials?",
      "type": "yes_no"
    },
    {
      "criterion": "Did the child record their observations accurately?",
      "type": "yes_no"
    }
  ]
}
```

### Discern Level (Anomaly Detection)

**SE2a-3A: Discern Variation A**
```json
{
  "capacity_id": "SE2a",
  "strand": 1,
  "band": 2,
  "cognitive_level": 3,
  "variation_id": "A",
  "task_type": "Discern (Anomaly Detection)",
  "risk_level": "Risk_Level_A",
  "safety_warning": "Safe for independent work. Do not eat unknown plants.",
  "scientific_materials": [
    "Ugandan fruit (e.g., jackfruit)",
    "leaves",
    "stone"
  ],
  "acceptable_alternatives": [
    "any local fruit",
    "grass",
    "wood"
  ],
  "parent_prompt": "Variation A: \"Tendo tried to do an experiment on Sensory Observation but did it backwards. Why did it fail?\"",
  "success_condition": "Child successfully completes the observation or explanation.",
  "failure_condition": "Child needs guidance. Parent asks guiding questions.",
  "reasoning_check": "What was the mechanical error?",
  "context_variants": {
    "default": {
      "names": [
        "Alex",
        "Sam",
        "Pat"
      ],
      "settings": [
        "park",
        "school",
        "store"
      ],
      "food": [
        "apples",
        "bread",
        "milk"
      ]
    },
    "ug": {
      "names": [
        "Amara",
        "Tendo",
        "Azie"
      ],
      "settings": [
        "Kampala market",
        "village",
        "garden",
        "savanna",
        "wetland"
      ],
      "food": [
        "matooke",
        "mangoes",
        "chapati",
        "jackfruit"
      ]
    }
  },
  "repetition_arc": {
    "execution_count": 3,
    "endurance": "noise_injection",
    "milestone": "M"
  },
  "worldview_connection": "Mechanism: Understanding how Sensory Observation works physically. Stewardship: We must know the true mechanism to care for it properly, not just guess."
}
```

### Own Level (Model Building & Stewardship)

**SE2a-4A: Own Variation A**
```json
{
  "capacity_id": "SE2a",
  "strand": 1,
  "band": 2,
  "cognitive_level": 4,
  "variation_id": "A",
  "task_type": "Own (Model Building & Stewardship)",
  "risk_level": "Risk_Level_A",
  "safety_warning": "Safe for independent work. Do not eat unknown plants.",
  "scientific_materials": [
    "Ugandan fruit (e.g., jackfruit)",
    "leaves",
    "stone"
  ],
  "acceptable_alternatives": [
    "any local fruit",
    "grass",
    "wood"
  ],
  "parent_prompt": "Variation A: \"Design a solution for our home using what you know about Sensory Observation. Build a model using Ugandan fruit (e.g., jackfruit), leaves, stone.\"",
  "success_condition": "Child successfully completes the observation or explanation.",
  "failure_condition": "Child needs guidance. Parent asks guiding questions.",
  "reasoning_check": "Explain your model and stewardship choice.",
  "context_variants": {
    "default": {
      "names": [
        "Alex",
        "Sam",
        "Pat"
      ],
      "settings": [
        "park",
        "school",
        "store"
      ],
      "food": [
        "apples",
        "bread",
        "milk"
      ]
    },
    "ug": {
      "names": [
        "Amara",
        "Tendo",
        "Azie"
      ],
      "settings": [
        "Kampala market",
        "village",
        "garden",
        "savanna",
        "wetland"
      ],
      "food": [
        "matooke",
        "mangoes",
        "chapati",
        "jackfruit"
      ]
    }
  },
  "repetition_arc": {
    "execution_count": 3,
    "endurance": "noise_injection",
    "milestone": "M"
  },
  "model_type": "Diagrammatic",
  "parent_rubric": [
    {
      "criterion": "Did the child build a functional model or clear prediction?",
      "type": "yes_no"
    },
    {
      "criterion": "Did the child explain the mechanism before the stewardship meaning?",
      "type": "yes_no"
    }
  ],
  "worldview_connection": "Mechanism: Accurate application of Sensory Observation. Stewardship: Using this knowledge to improve or protect our local environment/home."
}
```

## SE2f: Control Variables (Fair Test)

### Milestone Task

**LS2l-M: Milestone Production**
